<p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><b>Item
8.01. Other Events</b></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">On November
14, 2019,&#160;IBM received notification of an unsolicited &#8220;mini-tender&#8221; offer by Novus First Inc. (&#8220;NFI&#8221;),
dated November 11, 2019, to purchase up to 40,000 shares of IBM&#8217;s common stock, which is approximately 0.0045% of the 885,637,454
shares outstanding as of September 30, 2019, at a price of $111.00 per share in cash. NFI&#8217;s offer price is approximately
19.34% less than the $137.61 closing price of IBM&#8217;s common stock on the New York Stock Exchange on November 8, 2019, the
last trading day before the mini-tender offer commenced.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">IBM
does not endorse NFI&#8217;s mini-tender offer and recommends that IBM stockholders do not tender their shares in response to
the offer because the offer is at a price below the current market price for IBM&#8217;s shares. &#160;IBM urges stockholders
to obtain current market quotes for their shares, to review the conditions to NFI&#8217;s mini-tender offer, to consult with their
brokers or financial advisors and to exercise caution with respect to this mini-tender offer. IBM is not associated with NFI,
its mini-tender offer or the offer documentation.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Mini-tender
offers are designed to seek to acquire less than 5 percent of a company&#8217;s outstanding shares, thereby avoiding many disclosure
and procedural requirements of the Securities and Exchange Commission (&#8220;SEC&#8221;) that apply to offers for more than 5
percent of a company&#8217;s outstanding shares. As a result, mini-tender offers do not provide investors with the same level
of protection as provided by larger tender offers under United States federal securities laws.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">The
SEC has cautioned investors about these offers, noting that &#8220;[s]ome bidders make mini-tender offers at below-market prices,
hoping that they will catch investors off guard if the investors do not compare the offer price to the current market price.&#8221;
The SEC&#8217;s Tips for Investors regarding mini-tender offers may be found on the SEC&#8217;s website at <span style="text-decoration: underline">www.sec.gov/investor/pubs/minitend.htm<span style="color: blue">.</span></span></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">IBM
encourages brokers and dealers, as well as other market participants, to review the SEC&#8217;s letter regarding broker-dealer
mini-tender offer dissemination and disclosures at <span style="text-decoration: underline">www.sec.gov/divisions/marketreg/minitenders/sia072401.htm</span> and NASD&#8217;s
Notice to Members 99-53, issued July&#160;1999, regarding guidance to members forwarding mini-tender offers to their customers,
which can be found at <span style="text-decoration: underline">www.finra.org/web/groups/industry/@ip/@reg/@notice/documents/notices/p004221.pdf<span style="color: blue">.</span></span></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">IBM
requests that a copy of this 8-K be included with all distributions of materials relating to NFI&#8217;s mini-tender offer.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">IBM&#8217;s
web site (<span style="text-decoration: underline">www.ibm.com</span>) contains a significant amount of information about IBM, including financial and other information
for investors (<span style="text-decoration: underline">www.ibm.com/investor</span>/). IBM encourages investors to visit its various web sites from time to time, as information
is updated and new information is posted.</span></p>

e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
